I couldn't agree more with that statement.  <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/madebyanonymous\">Anonymous Singapore</a> made a book containing a selection of their work for potential clients. They also made that a case study of beautiful editorial design worth of being featured here on the blog. Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/motion-design-town-portal-vanitas\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_vanitas.jpg\" width=\"730\" height=\"596\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>10.26.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/gabrielecalvi\">Gabriele Calvi</a> shared a motion design project for the music video made for Vanitas is a free interpretation of a common sleep cycle with the aim of visually representing the dark and eerie sounds of the song. Hence the choice of the subject of “sleep” which, conceived as the most death-like everyday experience, allowed to trace the obscure and nocturnal atmosphere of the track, without sticking too much to the usual imagery associated with heavy music.</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>Anatomical representations, abstract settings, folkloristic figures, nightmares and still lives ( vanitas ) follow one another unceasingly to emphasize the complex structure of the song by creating continuous rhythmic-visual correspondences.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p>A journey where the protagonist and his consciousness ( the red sphere ) go through the five phases of sleep, from falling asleep to the catharsis of the REM phase, interrupted by an experience of sleep paralysis and followed by a turbulent awakening that brings the protagonist back to reality, in the dawn of a generic city in a day like any other.</p>\n\n<p>Listen to Town Portal <a href=\"https://townportal.bandcamp.com/\">here</a></p>\n\n<div xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>10.26.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/unitedby\">united by</a> shared an incredible branding, graphic design and visual identity project for the Y_Desenhar Portugal exhibition, an expo of Portuguese Design based on the conviction that Design schools are existential laboratories and observatories focused on the technology, sociology and aesthetics of Design, which demonstrate the diversity of perspectives and values in Design teaching. </p>\n\n<p>The invitation sent out to schools to take part in a critical Design exhibition, selecting projects carried out in the previous three years, led to a collection of 142 projects that showcase the ever-increasing variety of Design discussions and concerns. They seem to want to expand to fit knowledge, which leads to the creation of a veritable x-ray of the kind of Design that is taught and fostered in Portugal, as an expression of local consciousness and involvement.</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>\"In our observation of the radicals of Design we find design that is divided between a particular designer, an intention (to change) and technical means (to represent it). That is why we designed the exhibition as a “Y”, which has three converging lines: the lines of authorship, the program and the technology; but also, because “Y” identifies the generation celebrated in this biennial.\" - Francisco Providência</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img Foundation\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/branding-and-visual-identity-menomadin-foundation-2\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/7-posters_01_1.png\" width=\"2135\" height=\"969\" alt=\"Branding and Visual Identity for the Menomadin Foundation\" title=\"Branding and Visual Identity for the Menomadin Foundation\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>10.27.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>The fine folks from <a href=\"https://www.designit.com/\">Designit</a> are back with another case study covering their collaboration on the branding & visual identity for a non-profit <a href=\"https://menomadinfoundation.com/\">The Menomadin Foundation</a> and their 'mission-based' approach to social impact. Another project where Designit shines on how they approach through research to learn more through field research and our co-creation workshops. First of all, what strikes me the most from this brand identity is the logo for the Menomadin Foundation. It's clean, symmetrical with a twist but above all...timeless. Combined with beautiful photography, the color scheme simply aligns perfectly. Give it a look!</p>\n\n<h4>Links</h4>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://www.designit.com/\">https://www.designit.com/</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/designit/\">https://www.instagram.com/designit/</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/company/designit/\">https://www.linkedin.com/company/designit/</a></li>\n</ul><h2>In their words</h2>\n\n<blockquote>Blending strategic philanthropy, impact investments, and cross-sector partnerships, Menomadin takes a creative approach to doing good.</blockquote>\n\n<p><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/mYNUAm2yKcdqlrbDo6SEQTNaPltXqikGTIKOl-OxrF15YIDROupfGg7Ot1aRu4Gqb8fk8p415WpJAoRlLgRZp08UK9SSwCjSfDflIRfe3ib6vwx6pD547NH6v-mJha5aiYWFk7gN\" /></p>\n\n<h4>Process</h4>\n\n<p>Before diving into the branding and visual identity, we began by learning about their work in Luanda, Africa. Our team observed how they provide women and youth with the education and resources for financial independence. Through this field research and our co-creation meetings, we developed Menomadin’s blended business and financial model as a social impact foundation.</p>\n\n<h4>Concept</h4>\n\n<p>Menomadin begins by identifying the root causes of poverty and inequality in a region, then develops a cross-disciplinary and scalable solution that aligns with their profit goals and the United Nations’ Sustainable Development Goals. Together we defined the core terminology – strategic philanthropy, impact investing, and cross-sector partnerships – of how they help communities like Luanda. We then tailored their messaging to speak to different audiences. Once their organizational structure was determined, we designed their logo to emphasize their three-pronged approach. The natural color palette of their new website and print materials conveys the foundation’s goal of empowering people through sustainable efforts.</p>\n\n<p><img src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/uM2HYbhRxpRwab00LYbHJI4TAp0n4A-zh6XnCpUo5Jdm9ut0cgiadkT32Z-UW3MFTFPlYkLMSrEwZgzjdE_R9oe3XtmViQtReViZCnsZIVXRXTfdx8jek6s2sRy3IA5AVmUyApPD\" /></p>\n\n<p><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/WoWNaq_p0Q0SNenM6gR2ow0BkJU13QZapfcwW7dUxUTftZ5JBkkUZOwMhzgNoNFPCmkqSR3BpbMc-5CQJ6jUT4Yf0Vf0yoQ1GPpsTICAILVRaDixqC_eFQRYdSYF2TXBF_fH8Yg6\" /></p>\n\n<p><img Estudio</a> shared a beautiful branding and visual identity  for a digital advertising - programmatic company located in Madrid. The company is at a moment of big growth and national and international development. They were looking for updating their brand image with the values and strength necessary to go with the present moment. </p>\n\n<p>Starting from the concept of effervescence included in the world of the placebo, Marina and team have developed the brand identity. Another key has been to strengthen the brand with a more cosmopolitan than digital image, which on the other hand is their natural environment, acquiring a very personal and different image in the 00:53:57","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 00:53:57","title":"Shape our Future initiative - take part now for a better tomorrow","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/abduzeedo/~3/CsoulvIPZSU/shape-our-future-initiative-take-part-now-better-tomorrow","description":"Shape our Future initiative - take part now for a better tomorrow\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/shape-our-future-initiative-take-part-now-better-tomorrow\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/header_shapethefuture.png\" width=\"2880\" height=\"1600\" alt=\"Shape our Future initiative - take part now for a better tomorrow\" title=\"Shape our Future initiative - take part now for a better tomorrow\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>10.27.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>2020 is filled with events that will change the course of our lives for the years to come. Even though the year is still not over yet, there are things happening that need closer awareness in order to shape a better future. The kind folks from <a href=\"https://www.invisionapp.com/\">InVision</a> have kickstarted back in September what they called: 'Shape our Future' initiative. It's a campaign to incite us designers, artists, and makers to share what is our visual perspective of 'shaping the future' in the events of the upcoming US 2020 presidential election. I think we all share and passionate about this subject wherever we are on the globe, we have this ability to visually express a voice. Let's take part, together.</p>\n\n<blockquote>'Shape the Future' embodies more than just the act of voting. It is empowering enough to involve “change” in broad opportunities beyond just voting.</blockquote>\n\n<h3>Some notes</h3>\n\n<ul><li>You can stylize (or manipulate to a degree) the text but keep the integrity, legibility, and placement of the text.</li>\n\t<li>Export at 2000x2000 pixels at 72 ppi in RGB, saved as JPEG or PNG</li>\n\t<li>Write an artist’s statement (500 characters max) explaining how your illustration envisions your future.</li>\n</ul><h4>Links</h4>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSer08V1q_-_hN-7tI5LW_k8W32a7MtXAOX8_OdlX-8vrY074A/viewform\">Submit your artwork</a></li>\n</ul><h3 data-text-variant=\"heading-300\"><a
